<text>Love Love Love! We came here for my boyfriend's mom's birthday and they went above and beyond to celebrate the occasion - embarrassing slideshow and all!

The riddles were well made and engaging. We barely escaped!

What to expect:
- Arrive early by 15 mins to check in and sign waivers
- there is a lounge area when you first enter (this is the time to go to the bathroom)
- from there you're moved to another waiting room where there is a screen with instructions and the rules are explained by your guide
- then you're ushered to the lockers where you can put away your stuff and dress up!
- finally you are locked into your room and the time starts! (Okay, not really locked in; you can leave to go to the bathroom, but it's discouraged so go ahead of time)

We had a blast and the family who runs this place are just the sweetest. If we visit Napa again, we will definitely go again!</text>< rating>
5</rating>

< Review>
Delicious gourmet sandwiches.

I walked in on a Sunday afternoon and the first thing I noticed as I scanned the room were a sea of women in yoga pants and puffy jackets eating big ass bowls of salad. So in my yoga pants, I ordered a big ass sandwich instead. Stretchy waist band to the rescue.

No, I'm not spending over $15 on a salad! Granted I must admit they looked pretty good after watching the chefs in the back make them with their spread of freshly chopped ingredients. I'd rather spend my money on real food though...
Got pretty crowded - be prepared to share a table. Two single stalls of restrooms in the back.

Ordered:
Rooster Sandwich $13
Soft, freshly baked ciabatta bread with avocado, chipotle sauce, chicken, bacon and cheese. It was slightly toasted and it was friggin delicious.

With their expansive menu of sandwiches, I'd be back to try more.</Review>

I've never been disappointed by a burger here, and the starters are decent too.

Plusses:
- I went with a vegetarian friend who was quite impressed by his veggie burger and the list of vegetarian options
- The burgers are juicy and big, and the specialty ones are a good mix of seasoning - I get the hickory or caribbean

- You're a bit exposed in the outside seating area - no real block off from the sidewalk, no awning<//review>

< text>
Best takeout salads in SF and some of the best sandwiches as well (the rooster is excellent). More expensive than some alternatives, but blue barn gets all the details right. Extremely fresh (and local) ingredients, perfect balance of flavors, and just the right amount of dressing.

There will be lines. You will wait longer than you want for your food. You'll pay a few extra bucks for your salad/sando. Be patient... Or if the few extra bucks and/or the wait is too much to handle, then walk a couple blocks down the street to settle for shmeh at Plutos, where you can get a cheaper, more mediocre salad.</text>

< Review>
Good pizza and if you sign up for their text messages you can get some great deals on pizzas. I only had one problem with them though. There was a special for a three meat pizza that cost six or seven dollars. I said that I wanted one but asked if I could only have one meat on it, they said that wouldn't be the special and wanted to charge me nearly fourteen dollars. Really? You realize that you're saving money on the meat you aren't putting on the pizza, right?? I ended up not buying a single meat pizza for fourteen bucks. Next time I'll just get the special and take the meat off myself.

Come on people, think for yourselves. I know it's a special but I'm not asking for extras, I'm asking for less. That's better for your company. Think people, think.< /Review>

<review>I've had fairly bad experiences at dentist's offices. I have a very small mouth by nature, and I'd had dental assistants be quite disparaging and outright rude about having to work in my mouth. As a result I hadn't been to a dentist for an embarrassing amount of time before a friend recommended Dr. Qadeer's office to me. Any anxiety I had about the visit were gone as soon as I walked into the office. The office itself is lovely, as are the folks working there--every person is warm and inviting. And Dr. Qadeer himself is just the friendliest, most informative person you've ever met. He knew immediately ailments I was likely suffering from as a Type 1 Diabetic and provided me with an amazing amount of information and statistics about dental care with attention I've never received from another dentist. That first visit I discovered that I needed two root canals and had some cavities (that's what 5ish years away from the dentist will get you). The nervousness came back a little at mention of a root canal--was my small mouth going to be an issue again? < Review>
I have gotten a number of treatments done with all of the doctors at Mesa Dental and I would be lying if I said I was still afraid of the dentist!  Each experience has been quite pleasant to say the least.  Who gets to lay in a massage chair with a flat screen TV inches from your face while you're getting a filling?  I have probably fallen asleep in the chair its so comfortable!  Besides everyone in the office being so professional and friendly, each person in the office genuinely goes above and beyond so that you're in and out of there in no time, which is weird because its an office you would actually want to spend more time in! lol These sweet people deserve a raise!

Now if you're a big baby like myself, lets talk about the scary pain issue.  More like lack thereof! I don't know what their secret is, but I've never, EVER felt any pain or sensitivity in ANY of my appointments.  Not even in my root canals! (Yes, root canalSSS) After the first root canal expecting the worst, I was so surprised to not feel anything! Not even the initial needle for the anesthesia! I even begged for topical for that shot and they laughed at me :( So I clenched every muscle in my body to prepare and came to realized why they laughed. They knew exactly where to poke the needle and how to slowly ease the injection in my gums.  I was so comfortable, yes, comfortable, I wanted to take the tools and add more pressure to the scraping of my roots!  I know, TMI, but I have to be thorough.  In conclusion, eating a popsicle with my two front teeth hurts me more.

Thank you Mesa Dental for everything, you rock! <3< /Review>

I am pretty disappointed about this because I was comparing Extra Space and Public Storage. Both places advertised a 5 x 5, indoor, first floor units. Extra Space was actually more expensive but it was closer to my home so I went with them despite the price difference. I was pretty upset when I got to Extra Space and was told that my unit was actually on the top floor.

While this may seem like a minor detail, this is important to me because the items I will be storing in the unit are used seasonally, which means I will be in and out of the space carrying various items often. I wanted a ground unit so I could run in and run out quickly. I expressed this concern to Sara and she really tried to accommodate me. Since I had already signed the lease and brought my things over, I asked her to put me on the wait list in case anyone else moved out of a 5 x 5 on the first floor. <Review>I have been using Extra Space Storage off and on since 2008. My experience overall has been great. My reason for giving this particular location an "excellent " rating is simply due to the increased quality of costumer service and attention to detail about my needs. I am really working to get all of my items out of storage, however while I am working on that the staff, always greats my with a friendly greeting and are quick to get handle what my needs may be.
What finally lead me to write a review after all this time with extra space storage is attention to detail and awesome customer service provided to me by, the site manager LaTanya Bennett and Kathrine Weitherspoon, the assistant manager.
As many may know who have rented at this site for any long period of time, the merry-go-round of managerial changes has been quite frequent.
However, these two managers have done something no other manager has done for me, and that is look to save me money while also giving me the storage space I need. After a review of my account they were able to show me how I could achieve my storage goals while saving money at the same time. I have been well vested in Extra Space Storage for quite some time. And out of neccessity, have dealt with the cost, but not happy at all about what I had to incur for this amount of time. Yes, I was affected by the Real Estate market.
Nevertheless, I am taking this time out of my schedule to inform others. If you do need a storage facility, I would highly recommend this location.
Pro's- Informed Staff,Safe Location,Clean,Awesome internet deals
Con's- None, I have personally experienced(and I have no reason to be biased I am paying them they are not paying me :-) )<//Review>< Pictures>
